2026-03-23T16:16:06.3366274Z ##[group]Run # Note: There is currently no way to distinguish between undefined variables and empty strings in GitHub Actions.
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3367151Z [36;1m# Note: There is currently no way to distinguish between undefined variables and empty strings in GitHub Actions.[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3367806Z [36;1m# This limitation affects how we handle default values and empty inputs.[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3368332Z [36;1m# For more information, see: https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/924[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3368718Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3369085Z [36;1m# The following logic implements the configuration priority described in the README:[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3369498Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3369674Z [36;1m# Inputs[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3369885Z [36;1m# Environment Variables[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3370131Z [36;1m# Config File[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3370336Z [36;1m# Defaults[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3370524Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3370915Z [36;1m# As noted above defaults are awkward to handle as GitHub Actions will inject those values as the input[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3371572Z [36;1m# if the caller doesn't provide them, thus if the input matches the default we don't set it as we[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3372218Z [36;1m# can't tell the difference.  Plus if we did set it when it was the default value then it could potentially[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3373153Z [36;1m# override an external environment variable, or something in the callers configuration file, which then wouldn't[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3373846Z [36;1m# match the configuration priority that is documented.[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3374191Z [36;1mset_env_var_if_provided() {[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3374449Z [36;1m  local var_name="$1"[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3374690Z [36;1m  local input_value="$2"[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3374938Z [36;1m  local default_value="$3"[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3375170Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3375451Z [36;1m  if [ -n "$input_value" ] && [ "$input_value" != "$default_value" ]; then[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3375909Z [36;1m    # If action was provided with explicit input by the caller set that[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3376415Z [36;1m    # Use printf %q to safely escape special characters and prevent command injection[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3376917Z [36;1m    printf 'export %s=%q\n' "$var_name" "$input_value" >> trivy_envs.txt[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3377264Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3377439Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3377615Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-23T16:16:06.3377889Z [36;1m# Set environment variables, handling those with default values[0m
